        var reg = new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]*)(;|$)')
        var r = document.cookie.match(reg)
        return r ? unescape(r[2]) : null
      }

            if (!~qsIdx) {
              url = url + '?vt=' + now
            } else if (/vt=\d{8}/.test(url)) {
              url = url.replace(/vt=\d{8}/, 'vt=' + now)
            } else {
              var suffix = url.substring(qsIdx + 1)
              url = url.substring(0, qsIdx + 1) + 'vt=' + now
              if (suffix) url = url + '&' + suffix
            }
            history.pushState(null, document.title, url)
          }
        }, 300)
        document.removeEventListener('click', handleDocumentInitActive)
      }
      var el = document.querySelector('#bili-header-container')
      if (typeof BiliHeader !== 'undefined') {
        var header = new BiliHeader({
          config: {
            headerType: 'mini',
            forceVersion: 3,
            themeSwitch: getCookie('header_theme_version') === 'OPEN',
            useThemeOpen: true,
            disableSticky: true,
            tokenSupport: true,
          },
        })
        header.init(el)
      }
      var observer = new MutationObserver(function (mutationsList, observer) {
        for (var mutation of mutationsList) {
          if (mutation.type === 'attributes') {
            if (el.offsetHeight) {
              observer.disconnect()
              var elIc = document.querySelector('#i_cecream')
              elIc.style.minHeight = 'calc(100vh - ' + el.offsetHeight + 'px)'
            }
          }
        }
      })
      observer.observe(el, { attributes: true })
  </script>

  </script>
